PIE-95481 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
Option to include or exclude null values in OpenAPI responses.

After applying a fix that includes PIE-92557, Integration Server handles fields
with null values in a REST response differently. Prior to application of a fix 
that includes PIE-92557, Integration Server omits fields with null values in an 
OpenAPI response instead of returning them explicitly. PIE-92557 changed the 
behavior to always include null fields in the response. However, this resulted
in unexpected and unwanted behavior in some existing implementations.

To resolve this issue, the existing watt.server.rest.includeNullFieldsInResponse
server configuration parameter now controls whether an OpenAPI response 
includes null values. Set the parameter to true to include empty fields with 
null values in the REST response. Set to false to omit empty fields from 
the REST response.

PIE-95543 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
Integration Server ignores the timeout property for the Invoke flow step
during an HTTP client call.

When a flow service has an Invoke step to call the pub.client:http service and
the timeout property is configured for the step, Integration Server ignores the
timeout period while waiting for the pub.client:http service to complete. This
issue occurs for the following reasons: 
- A regression introduced in the resolution for the defect PIE-65495.
- The server relies on the read timeout instead of the INVOKE timeout when
reading the response from pub.client:http, which leads to failure in the case of
a slow stream. 

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-95675 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)

PIE-95691 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
Service ends with java.util.ConcurrentModificationException.

When a service completes, Integration Server executes cleanup logic for all of
the resources used by that service. An internal class manages the list of
resources and, upon service completion, a thread iterates through the list and
closes the resources one by one. If another thread accesses the list at the same
time, Integration Server throws a  java.util.ConcurrentModificationException. 

The clean-up logic is now thread-safe, ensuring that only one thread at a time
can access the resource list.

When a client sends a REST API POST request to Integration Server with query
parameters and a request body, Integration Server returns a response to the
client with the query parameters in the response body. However, the query
parameters should remain outside the response body. 

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-96170 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
Outbound SSL handshake is very slow and Integration Serve appears unresponsive.

When Integration Server is configured to reuse SSL sessions for outbound
requests (watt.security.ssl.resumeClientSessions=true), thread contention issues
cause the outbound SSL handshake to be very slow when there are multiple
concurrent outbound requests.  The thread contention resulted in an increase in
threads being blocked and Integration Server appeared to be unresponsive. 

This fix removes the cause of the thread contention, resulting in performance
improvements when there are multiple outbound SSL requests. 

PIE-96247 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
CATCH step does not catch the RuntimeException thrown by a flow service for the
"Transformers cannot loop over list elements" error. 

If a flow service contains a MAP step in which an incorrectly configured
transformer causes Integration Server to throw a "Transformers cannot loop
over list elements" error, Integration Server surfaces the error as a
RuntimeException. However, Integration Server should indicate that the error is
a FlowException as this error cannot be caught by a CATCH step. When a
FlowException occurs, Integration Server terminates the entire flow service
immediately. If the FlowException occurs in a TRY step, the following CATCH step
cannot catch the FlowException. This is by design. 

Integration Server now clarifies that the "Transformers cannot loop over list
elements" error is a FlowException wrapped in a RuntimeException. 

Prior to this fix, Integration Server produces the following error:

java.lang.RuntimeException: [ISC.0049.9027] Error at
pub.list:appendToDocumentList - Transformers cannot loop over list elements 

After this fix, Integration Server produces the following error to avoid the
confusion where this error is expected to be caught by the TRY/CATCH steps: 

java.lang.RuntimeException: com.wm.lang.flow.FlowException: [ISC.0049.9027]
Error at pub.list:appendToDocumentList - Transformers cannot loop over list
elements 

PIE-96248 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
In the pub.string:isNullEmptyOrWhitespace service, the ifPresent boolean input 
parameter is a text field in Designer.

Although Designer displays the ifPresent parameter as a text field,
Integration Server handles the parameter value as boolean. However, the
text field lets users enter a non-boolean value, which results in service
execution errors.

The issue is resolved. Now, Designer displays the parameter as a drop-down
field with only true or false as options.

PIE-96395 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)

PIE-96500 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
Integration Server experiences high CPU usage when Universal Messaging servers
are stopped in the Horizontal Scaling setup.

The high CPU usage is due to numerous Universal Messaging client sessions 
repeatedly attempting to reconnect to the stopped servers every 2 seconds.

This issue is resolved by distributing UM session re-connections over a period 
of time to prevent CPU spikes, using two newly introduced server configuration 
parameters:

    - watt.server.messaging.um.session.reconnectImmediately: Specifies whether 
      Integration Server reconnects immediately. Set the parameter to true for 
	  an immediate reconnection attempt or false to prevent the attempt. The 
	  default value is true.
    - watt.server.messaging.um.session.reconnectInterval: Specifies the interval 
	  at which Integration Server attempts an immediate reconnection. The 
	  default value is 5 seconds. There is no maximum value for this parameter. 
	  The reconnection interval is calculated as the set value plus a random 
	  value between 0 and the set value.
      For example, if there are 10 sessions, session 1 may have an interval of 5 
      seconds, session 2 may have 7 seconds, session 3 may have 9 seconds, and 
	  so on. This staggered retry mechanism prevents all sessions from 
	  reconnecting simultaneously, reducing CPU load.

You must restart Integration Server for changes to these parameters to take effect.

Integration Server becomes unresponsive during design time activities.

When Integration Server has a large number of nodes or elements 
in the packages, design time activities may become slow or unresponsive.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-96613 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
The jcode hailmary command returns the doesCompilationHasError flag as false 
even when package compilation has errors.

When you run the jcode hailmary command, if the compilation result has errors, 
the command returns the doesCompilationHasError flag as true. However, if the 
compilation result has errors and warnings, the doesCompilationHasError 
flag is false. This behaviour is because the jcode logic checks the last line 
of the compilation result to identify errors. When warnings are present, the 
jcode logic incorrectly picks up the warning text instead of the error text.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-96691 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix18)
Updates to the Integration Server license verification process for
transaction-based licenses. 

Beginning with application of a fix that includes PIE-96691, the license
verification process changes for transaction-based license. Specifically,
Integration Server no longer verifies the expiration date of a transaction-based
license. If you have a transaction-based license, you must install a fix that
includes PIE-96691 before your existing license key expires. 
 
Important! If you have a core-based license for Integration Server with an
expiration date that has passed or is about to pass, you need to replace your
existing license with a Generic License Key. The Generic License Key replaces
your existing license keys when your subscription term has expired and you have
renewed the subscription with IBM. Generic License Keys are available in an
archive that can be downloaded from https://www.ibm.com/support/fixcentral.  For
more information about installing and using Generic License Keys, review the
README_webMethods Keys.txt file included in the archive. 
 
If you are not sure whether your products are licensed based on Transactions or
cores, review your contract or contact your IBM Sales Representative for help. 

PIE-87487 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)
Integration Server throws java.lang.IndexOutOfBoundsException for some 
certificates used in an Enterprise Gateway configuration.

In an Enterprise Gateway configuration, when the internal Integration Server 
sends a certificate containing tab and newline characters 
(\r\n) to the registration port for authentication, the registration port treats 
"\r\n" as the end of the payload and fails to read the certificate, causing 
Integration Server to throw the exception.

The issue is now resolved by introducing the following server configuration 
parameter:

watt.server.enterprisegateway.cert.delimiter 
Specifies the characters that mark the end of the payload when the internal 
Integration Server sends a certificate to the Enterprise Gateway registration 
port for authentication. If the certificate includes tab and newline characters 
(\r\n), apply the fix with PIE-87487 to both the internal and Enterprise Gateway 
servers and set the parameter value to "$$". The default value is "\r\n".

Note: If you change the value of this property, you must disable and then enable
the Enterprise Gateway external port, Enterprise Gateway registration port, and 
the internal server port for the changes to take effect.

PIE-87951 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)

request, resulting in service failures.

When a client invokes a Swagger REST request after an OpenAPI REST request, 
Integration Server incorrectly treats the Swagger REST request as an OpenAPI
REST request. This results in Integration Server placing the wrong data in the 
pipeline, which leads to service failure.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-92298 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)
Changes for watt.client.data.maxToStringLength server configuration parameter.

The watt.client.data.maxToStringLength parameter specifies the maximum length of
the String produced by IData.toString(). When the maximum String length is
reached, Integration Server crops the value and adds an ellipses "..." at the
end. This fix introduces the following changes to the property: 

- The default value is now 65536.
- If the parameter is set to a value greater than 65536, Integration Server
writes a message to the server log at start up warning of potential performance
problems. Note that the performance of IData.toString() decreases as the value
of watt.client.data.maxToStringLength increases. 
- The minimum value is now 200. If the parameter is set to a value less than
200, Integration Server logs a message about the minimum and resets the
parameter to 200.

PIE-93870 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)

PIE-94220 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)
Rebuilding the Apache Lucene document repository used by the Statistics Data
Collector may negatively impact performance. 

When the Apache Lucene document repository used by the Statistics Data Collector
is purged, Integration Server rebuilds by executing an unbounded SQL select of
metrics data. When the number of rows in the database is large, executing the
unbounded query can place a heavy load on the database and negatively impact
performance. 

Now, Integration Serve rebuilds the repository by executing a collection of
bounded batches of SQL rows, which ensure the number of results for each query
is limited. 

The Apache Lucene document repository is located at:
<install>/IntegrationServer/instances/<instanceName>/monitorRepo/core/index 

PIE-94291 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)

despite being configured to reload without dependent packages.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-94301 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)
Changes to handling of OAuth authorization codes.

Integration Server generates OAuth authorization codes and stores the codes in
cache. After Integration Server issues a bearer token to an OAuth client in
exchange for the authorization code, Integration Server removes the
authorization code from cache. Integration Server executes the Remove Expired
AuthCodes system task to remove unused expired authorization codes from cache.
The watt.server.oauth.authCode.expirySeconds server configuration parameter
determines the frequency with which the system task executes. 

This fix also includes internal changes for supporting OAuth with layered
products.

PIE-94519 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)
Configuration variables does not provide a way to specify the order in which
LDAP directories are searched. 

An Integration Server can be configured to search multiple LDAP directories for
user authentication. The order in which the LDAP directories are listed on the
Security > User management > LDAP configuration page in Integration Server
Administrator determines the order in which Integration Server searches the LDAP
directories for a user. While configuration variables (application.properties)
can be used to define an LDAP directory for an Integration Server, it does not
provide a way to specify the order in which Integration Server searches the LDAP
directories. As a result, Integration Server searches the LDAP server entries in
an arbitrary order. 

To resolve this issue, this fix introduces the configuration variable:
ldap.<uuid>.order. Use this variable to indicate the order in which Integration
Server creates and searches LDAP directories for a matching user during
authentication. Integration Server creates LDAP directories in ascending order,
starting with 1. If two or more LDAP directories are assigned the same order
number, Integration Server creates the LDAP directories with the same number in
an arbitrary order. If an LDAP directory is not assigned an order number,
Integration Server creates the directory after creating directories with an
order number. Integration Server searches the LDAP directories in the same order
in which it creates them.

In rare cases, the internal service used to log out of a session ends with a
NullPointerException. 

This issue is now resolved.

Apache Lucene regular expression denial of service
https://exchange.xforce.ibmcloud.com/vulnerabilities/216835 

The new libraries are:
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-core:8.11.3
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-grouping:8.11.3
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-queryparser:8.11.3
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-analyzers-common:8.11.3
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-suggest:8.11.3
 
The old libraries are:
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-core:8.10.1
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-grouping:8.9.0
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-queryparser:8.10.1
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-analyzers-common:8.10.1
- org.apache.lucene:lucene-suggest:8.9.0

PIE-94586 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)
In Integration Server 10.15, SFTP login fails when the Integration Server
attempts to reuse an existing SFTP session to connect to the SFTP server.

After migrating from 10.11 to 10.15, running the pub.client.sftp:login service
with reuseSession parameter set to true results in the error:
Cannot invoke "com.sshtools.sftp.SftpClient.cd(String)" because the return value
of "com.wm.app.b2b.server.sftp.client.SFTPSession.getSftpClient()" is
null.

This issue arises when a logged-in user navigates to a directory other than
the home directory. The session retains the current directory information,
which the service mistakenly treats as the default directory for subsequent
logins using the same session. Consequently, Integration Server fails to log
in to the SFTP server.

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server introduces the
"watt.server.sftp.resetHomeDir" parameter that determines the user's default
default directory upon login. By default, the parameter is false. Set the
parameter to true to ensure that the user's home directory is always the default
directory upon login.

You need not restart Integration Server for the changes to the parameter
to take effect.

PIE-94635 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix17)

PIE-88449 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix16)

PIE-92339 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix16)
Ability to control the use of pretty print formatting for the 
pub.xml:documentToXMLString service.

By default, Integration Server uses pretty print formatting for the output of 
the pub.xml:documentToXMLString service. Pretty print uses new lines and 
indentation to make the XML String more readable in a text editor. This 
formatting might be superfluous for some situations.

To control the use or pretty print formatting for the XML String produced by 
the pub.xml:documentToXMLString, Integration Server now includes a server 
configuration parameter to set the global default value and a new service input 
parameter to control the formatting an a per service basis.

watt.server.xml.prettyPrint
Specifies whether pretty print formatting is the default for the XML String 
produced by the pub.xml:documentToXMLString service. When set to true, the 
pub.xml:documentToXMLString formats the XML String with new lines and 
indentation to make the XML more readable when viewed in a text editor. When set 
to false, the pub.xml:documentToXMLString does not use new lines or indentations. 
The default is true.

Integration Server does not need to be restarted for changes to this parameter 
to take effect.

pub.xml:documentToXMLString input
prettyPrint - String. Optional. Flag indicating whether the service performs 
pretty print formatting for the XML String returned in the xmldata output. 
Pretty print uses new lines and indentation to make the XML String more readable 
in a text editor. Set to:

- true to perform pretty print formatting
- false to not use pretty print formatting
- <none> - to use the value specified by the watt.server.xml.prettyPrint server 
configuration parameter to determine if pretty print formatting is performed.
 
There is no default value for this input parameter.

PIE-94018 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix16)
Changes to Integration Server to address vulnerability to Server-Side Request
Forgery (SSRF) attack. 

Integration Server can now be configured to perform SSRF checking on outbound
server connections. Integration Server provides server configuration parameters
that can be used to enable SSRF checking on direct connections and redirect
connections. 

watt.net.http.connect.performSSRFcheck: Specifies whether SSRF checking is
performed for direct outbound connections. When SSRF checking is performed for
direct outbound connections, Integration Server verifies that the host to which
the request is being sent is on the allow list established by the
watt.net.http.ssrf.allowlist parameter. If the host is not on the allow list,
Integration Server rejects the request with the error "Connection to URL {0} is
not permitted." Set to true to enable SSRF checking for direct outbound
connections. Set to false to disable SSRF checking for direct outbound
connections. The default is false. A value of true is more secure. 

Integration Server restart is required for changes to this parameter to take
effect. 

watt.net.http.redirect.performSSRFcheck: Specifies whether SSRF checking is
performed for redirected outbound connections. When SSRF checking is performed
for redirected outbound connections, Integration Server verifies that the host
to which the request is being redirected is on the allow list established by the
watt.net.http.ssrf.allowlist parameter. If the host is not on the allow list,
Integration Server rejects the request with the error "Redirection to URL {url}
is not permitted." Set to true to enable SSRF checking for redirected outbound
requests. Set to false to disable SSRF checking for redirected outbound
requests. The default is false. A value of true is more secure. 

Integration Server restart is required for changes to this parameter to take
effect. 

watt.net.http.ssrf.allowlist: Specifies a comma-delimited list of regex
expressions for allowed host names for SSRF checking. If SSRF checking is
enabled for direct outbound connections and/or redirected outbound connections,
the host name to which the direct or redirected outbound request is being sent
must appear in the allow list established by this parameter. This parameter is
empty by default. 

Integration Server restart is required for changes to this parameter to take
effect. 

PIE-94301 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix16)
Changes to handling of OAuth authorization codes.

Integration Server generates OAuth authorization codes and stores the codes in
cache. After Integration Server issues a bearer token to an OAuth client in
exchange for the authorization code, Integration Server removes the
authorization code from cache. Integration Server executes the Remove Expired
AuthCodes system task to remove unused expired authorization codes from cache.
The watt.server.ouath.authCode.expireSeconds system task determines the
frequency with which the system task executes. 

This fix also includes internal changes for supporting OAuth with layered
products.

PIE-94985 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix16)
In a horizontal scalability setup, when one Universal Messaging (UM) node goes 
down, the Client Side Queue (CSQ) count for the webMethods messaging connection 
alias on Microservices Runtime increases.
 
Consider that Integration Server uses a Universal Messaging horizontal scalability 
URL (for example, (UM1)(UM2)(UM3)) as the Realm URL in the webMethods Messaging 
Connection Alias configuration. In this scenario, instead of routing messages to 
the remaining UM nodes in the horizontal scalability setup, the server queues the 
messages in the CSQ, which increases the CSQ count.
 
This issue is resolved by setting the watt.server.um.producer.transaction.commitRetryCount
server configuration parameter to a value greater than 0. For more information 
on the parameter, see IBM webMethods Integration Server Administrator's Guide.

Integration as of September 13th, 2024.

PIE-84703 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
In a repository-based deployment, custom Access Control Lists (ACLs) with 
allow/deny groups are installed correctly on the target server, but the 
associated group assignments are missing after deployment.

When deploying an ACL with allow/deny groups through a repository-based 
deployment, the ACL gets installed on the target server, but the associated 
group assignments are missing. The issue occurs because the deployment requires 
the groups to be present on both the build and target servers to create these 
associations. If the groups exist only on the target server, the ACL cannot be  
associated with the groups.

The issue is now resolved by introducing the following server configuration 
parameter:

watt.server.asset.build.enforceAclGroupAssociation
Specifies if custom ACLs deployed through a repository-based deployment include 
allow/deny groups on the target server, even if these groups are missing from 
the build server. However, you must manually add the "properties.cnf" 
configuration file with the setting
watt.server.asset.build.enforceAclGroupAssociation=true 
in the source repository folder alongside the other configuration files.
When set to true, the Asset Build Environment generates the ACDL and ZIP files, 
with ACLs that include the allow/deny group associations, regardless of whether 
the groups are available on the build server. When set to false or if the 
properties.cnf file is empty or missing from the source repository, the ACLs 
exclude the allow/deny group associations if the groups are absent from the 
build server.

Integration Server restart is not required for changes to the parameter to 
take effect.

PIE-87127 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server instance creation fails when fixes cannot be installed but

instance and applies any existing fixes. However, the is_instance script only 
installs fixes if "sum.install.dir" is provided or if Update Manager is part
of the Integration Server installation. If the fixes cannot be installed, the
instance creation fails. Because installing fixes is an optional part of instance
creation, failure to install fixes should not prevent the is_instance script 
from successfully creating an instance.

This issue is now resolved. Instance creation no longer fails if fixes cannot be 
applied to a new instance.

PIE-88272 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Addition of server configuration parameter to prevent a deadlock when the
Statistics Data Collector inserts metrics. 

When the Statistics Data Collector inserts metrics data into the database and
the transaction hangs indefinitely, it can lead to high thread usage in
Integration Server which can adversely affect performance. This could occur if a
database table needed for the completion of the metrics data transaction is
locked by another process. 

To prevent this potential deadlock, Integration Server now includes the
following server configuration parameter for setting a timeout for data
insertion: 

watt.server.statisticsDataCollector.dbInsert.secsTimeout
Specifies the number of seconds that the Statistics Data Collector waits when
attempting to insert metrics into the database. After the timeout elapses,
Integration Server writes a debug level message to the server log about the
timeout and discards the metrics event. Once the insertion timeout occurs, the
Statistics Data Collector writes metrics to memory until the database issue
resolves or the Statistics Data Collector is disabled. After the database issue
resolves, the Statistics Data Collector inserts the queued events into the
database. Set to a positive integer or 0 (zero). A value of 0 indicates that
there is no timeout and the Statistics Data Collector will wait indefinitely to
complete the transaction for inserting metrics into the database. The default is
15 seconds. 

Do not specify a timeout value greater than the statistics data collection
interval as this may cause thread utilization for the Statistics Data Collector
to increase. The statistics data collection interval is determined by the
watt.server.stats.pollTime and has a default value of 60 seconds. 

Integration Server does not need to be restarted for changes to this parameter
to take effect. 

PIE-88346 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Journal events are not being logged.

The Event Manager in Integration Server invokes event handlers that subscribe to
specific types of events. However, Integration Server did not log Journal
events, preventing execution of event handlers that subscribed to Journal
events. 

This issue is now resolved. 

PIE-88454 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
New thread dump log utility to create thread dumps that contain additional
information useful for debugging. 
 
Integration Server can now generate a thread dump log that contains additional
information, including: 
 
- The name of the service executing the thread.
- CPU time used by the thread since the JVM started.
- Amount of memory currently allocated by the thread.
- Any JDBC pool connections the thread might hold.
 
When the thread dump reporting utility is enabled, Integration Server
automatically generates the thread dump reports when one of the following
occurs: 
- The JDBC function pool does not have any available connections
- The percentage of available threads in the server thread pool drops below the
watt.server.control.serverThreadThreshold value. 
- The percentage of available stateful sessions in the session pool drops below
the watt.server.session.stateful.warning value 
 
After one of the above events occurs, Integration Server produces the following
sequence of reports: 
 
1. An initial full thread dump report
2. 30 seconds later another full thread dump report is created
3. 30 seconds later another full thread dump report is created.
 
Integration Server writes the thread dump reports  to the following log file:

<IntegrationServer_installDirectory>/instances/<instanceName>/logs/diagnostics/
tdump-<yyyy><dd><mm>-<ss>-pid<processID>.log
 
Integration Server writes messages to the wrapper.log when a thread dump log is
created, for example: 
 
INFO   | jvm 1    | 2024/05/13 07:39:14 | Produced thread dump. 
INFO   | jvm 1    | 2024/05/13 07:39:14 | Reason: Received signal to dump
threads 
INFO   | jvm 1    | 2024/05/13 07:39:14 | 
INFO   | jvm 1    | 2024/05/13 07:39:14 | Created thread dump file:
/IntegrationServer/instances/default/logs/diagnostics/tdump-2024-05-13_07-39-14-pid2870580.log
 
After Integration Server creates a set of thread dump logs, at least 10 minutes
must pass before one of the conditions discussed above will trigger another set
of thread dump logs. This interval is not configurable. 
 
Integration Server limits the disk space used by thread dump logs by setting a
disk quota of 50 MB.  After 50 MB have been allocated to thread dump longs, when
the next thread dump is triggered, Integration Server compresses all existing
thread dump log files before producing the new log.  After Integration Server
has created 50 MB of compressed thread dump logs, when the next thread dump is
triggered, Integration Server deletes the second oldest compressed file for a
thread dump from disk before creating a new log. 
 
Integration Servers uses sever configuration parameters to enable the generation
of thread dump logs and control the use of the service names in the logs. 
 
watt.server.diagnostic.threadDumper  
Whether the thread dump logging utility is enabled. Set to true to generate a
series of thread dumps when Integration Server encounters resource level limits
identified above. Set to false to disable the thread dump logger utility. The
default is true. 
 
Integration Server does not need to be restarted for changes to this parameter
to take effect. 
 
Integration Server writes the following to the wrapper log when the utility is
enabled: 
> INFO   | jvm 1    | 2024/05/12 13:36:08 | Registered custom signal handler for
thread dumper. (kill -USR1 2870580) 
 
Integration Server writes the following to the wrapper log when the utility is
disabled: 
> INFO   | jvm 1    | 2024/05/13 07:42:45 | Unregistered custom signal handler
for thread dumper. 
 
Note: The archive created by the diagnostic collector includes the generated
thread dump files. 
 
watt.server.diagnostic.threadNameWithService
Whether or not the thread dump report includes the fully qualified name of the
Integration Server service executing on the thread. Set to true to include the
service name in the report. The utility prepends the name of the executing
service to the name of the service originally executing on the thread. After
service invocation completes, the name of service is removed from subsequent
report entries. Only the original service name remains. 
 
Additionally, when this parameter is set to true, if a socket is bound to the
current InvokeState, the utility includes it's full address is included with the
name of the fully qualified service. Below is an example entry in the report for
the wm.server:ping service. The service connected to port 5555 using local port
56438. 
 
[tid=368]
wm.server:ping-174-_Socket[addr=/192.168.64.1,port=56438,localport=5555]
[state=RUNNABLE] 
Set this parameter to false if you do not want report entries to include the
name of the service currently executing on the thread. Only the name of the
service originally invoked with the thread will be included. 
 
The default is true.
 
Integration Server must be restarted for changes to this parameter to take
effect. 
 
Note: The thread dump logs may be explicitly triggered for non-Windows platforms
by using the 'kill 'command from a terminal shell.  Send 'kill -USR1 <pid>'
There is no limit on the number or timing of thread dumps created in this
manner. When watt.server.diagnostic.threadDumper=true, Integration Server also
creates a thread dump log when the  'kill -USR1 <pid>'  command is sent. 
 
Important!  Sending this command to an Integration Server that has
watt.server.diagnostic.threadDumper set to false, causes the JVM to exit.  In
this situation, use the 'kill -3 <pid>' or  create a diagnostic zip instead.
However, these alternatives result in Java's standard thread dump report. The
additional information provided by the thread dump logging utility will not be
included. 
 
PIE-88566 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
The pub.xml:queryXMLNode service trims leading and trailing whitespaces
in the query result.

The service must return the content of the queried field in the XML node
without modifications. However, the service trims the spaces around the
field content.

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server provides the
watt.client.node.trimBlanks server configuration parameter, which determines
whether the service trims the leading and trailing whitespaces or retains them.
Set the parameter to false to retain and true to trim the white spaces.
The default value for the parameter is true.

You do not need to restart the server for changes to the parameter to take
effect.

to appear in the Docker images.

PIE-92579 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)

PIE-92595 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server throws UnsupportedMediaTypeException when handling an OpenAPI 
REST request with Accept header that contains a wildcard or a combination of 
media types.

Consider a REST API Descriptor (RAD) created as a provider from an OpenAPI 
document, and the OpenAPI document can have multiple HTTP status codes in an 
operation response. Each HTTP status code can have various media types defined. 
For instance, consider that the HTTP status code 200 might include both 
application/json and application/xml. If a request has an Accept header value 
of */ * or a combination of media types (for example, Accept: application/json,
application/xml), and the response is 200, Integration Server throws 
UnsupportedMediatypeException.

This issue is resolved. Now, if a request has an Accept header value with a 
wild card or combination of media types, the response defaults to the first 
matching media type.

PIE-92825 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)

When converting a JSON string to a document (an IData object) 
using the pub.json:jsonStringToDocument service in Integration Server
Administrator, the pub.json:jsonStringToDocument service fails 
if you do not specify jsonDocumentTypeName, even though jsonDocumentTypeName is
an optional parameter. 

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-92842 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server experiences memory issues (high resource and memory 
consumption) during design time activities such as copy, paste, rename, and so
on. 

Designer and webMethods.io show slow response times during design time
activities such as copy, paste, rename, and so on with hundreds of document type
references, resulting in high resource and memory consumption. 

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server performs better by optimizing
the flow service operations to minimize memory usage. 

PIE-92849 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
New default value for the indexInterval parameter which determines how often the
Statistics Data Collector queries the database for new results and creates
Lucene documents. 

The indexInterval parameter now has a default value of 90 seconds. Previously,
the default value was 300 seconds.  However, Integration Server will not set the
parameter to the new default if the indexInterval value was changed from the
default. 

The indexInterval parameter is located in
<install_directory>/IntegrationServer/instances/<instanceName>/config/monitor/monitor.cnf.

PIE-92928 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server returns an "HTTP 404 Not Found" error to
an OpenAPI request with "/" as the operation path.

For an OpenAPI request with "/" as the operation path,
Integration Server returns the "HTTP 404 Not Found" error instead
of the expected response.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-92959 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
In Integration Server 10.15 with the latest fix, the pub.cache:removeAll
service fails to remove the specified keys.

The pub.cache:removeAll service removes all elements from the cache
when keys are not specified. However, when keys are passed,
the specified elements are not removed.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-92978 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Resolution for OutOfMemoryExceptions that may occur during debugging and while
decoding a JSON message. 

This fix addresses two situations in which OutOfMemeoryExceptions may be
observed. 

- While using Designer to debug steps in a flow service, if the pipeline
contains a very large, nested document mapped to a variable, Designer may throw
an OutOfMemoryException. To resolve this issue, Designer does not transform all
values into a String during a debugging session.  Designer only transforms the
value of variables relevant to the debug session. 

- When decoding a JSON string into a document (IData object), Integration Server
throws an OutOfMemoryException. To avoid this situation, Integration Server now
releases memory as soon as possible once the JSON string has been transformed
into a document. 

PIE-93029 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
NullPointerException occurs when
com.wm.app.b2b.server.ProtocolState.getDirective executes . 

If com.wm.app.b2b.server.ProtocolState.getDirective executes and the directive
is not present, Integration Server throws a NullPointerException. Integration
Server should handle the situation more gracefully. 

Now, Integration Server no longer throws a NullPointerException when
com.wm.app.b2b.server.ProtocolState.getDirective executes and the directive is
not present. 

PIE-93055 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server experiences performance degradation when
parsing large JSON text after upgrading Jackson libraries.

After upgrading the Jackson libraries to 2.16.x, Integration Server
slows down significantly when parsing large JSON text.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-93066 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
The timeout value set for the pub.client:http service is not being honored when
sending to an https endpoint. 

When the pub.client:http service sends a request to an https endpoint and the
request times out, the actual timeout value is always twice the duration
specified in the timeout input parameter. 

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-93124 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server intermittently throws a java.net.SocketException.

For an Integration Server on which API Gateway runs, Integration Server
intermittently throws the following exception under high request load
conditions. 

java.net.SocketException: Socket output is already shutdown

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-93139 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server incorrectly logs the payload of a POST API request
for the subsequent GET API request when an HTTP interceptor is in use.

The issue occurs because Integration Server reuses the socket connection
created for a request in subsequent requests when the Connection header is
'keep-alive', and does not update the payload until a new payload is received.
Therefore, when an HTTP interceptor intercepts a GET request, Integration Server
logs the payload from the previous POST request for the GET request.

This issue is now resolved. When an HTTP interceptor is in use,
Integration Server refreshes the socket connection for each request regardless
of the Connection header in the request.

PIE-93142 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server fails to convert date or time using the
pub.date:dateTimeFormat service, if invoked from an external application. 

When using the pub.date:dateTimeFormat service from anywhere 
other than Designer, the service throws an error because the locale parameter
value is passed as an empty string. 

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-93151 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
OpenID authentication process returns a 401 Unauthorized status when the OpenID
Provider is an Entra ID instance and the value of token_endpoint_auth_method on
the provider is "private_key_jwt". 

When the OpenID Provider is an Entra ID instance and the provider's
token_endpoint_auth_method is "private_key_jwt", the OpenID authentication
process returns a 401 Unauthorized status. This happens because Entra ID
requires the signature header in the JWT to contain the x5t and typ fields.
Integration Server does not include the fields in the header of the JWT
signature. These fields are defined as optional in the Java Web Signature
standard, but are required by Entra ID. 

This issue is resolved. If the configured OpenID Provider's issuer value
contains "microsoft," Integration Server includes the x5t and typ fields in the
header of the JWT signature. 

PIE-93180 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
SOAP handler services are generating metering data but should not.

This issue is resolved. webMethods Metering no longer generates metering data
for SOAP handler services. 

PIE-93193 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Insufficient information in Integration Server diagnostics.

In Integration Server, the diagnostic utility does not include all 
the details about the runtime information of the webMethods 
messaging trigger.

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server includes all the 
details about the runtime data information of webMethods 
triggers in the diagnostics.

PIE-93791 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Metering.csv file is created even when the metering simulator is disabled.

When watt.server.metering.simulator.enabled is set to false, the metering
simulator is disabled. Integration Server creates the metering.csv file when the
metering simulator is disabled but should not. 
 
This issue is now resolved.

PIE-93840 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
In flat file processing, a request without a body no longer results in an null
ffdata object being added to the pipeline. 
 
After applying a fix or upgrading to a release that includes PIE-84414, when
Integration Server receives a flat file request without a body (payload), a null
ffdata object is not added to the pipeline as it was before. The change for
PIE-84414 resolves an issue where a SocketTimeOutException occurred for requests
that did not have a body and the request specified one of the following
Content-Types: application/x-www-form-urlencoded, application/xml, and text/xml.
However, this change is not needed for all Content-Types and can cause issues in
existing implementations that relied on the old behavior. 
 
To resolve this issue, Integration Server now includes a server configuration
parameter to process empty payloads for specific Content-Types. 
 
watt.server.content.type.processEmptyPayload
Specifies a comma-separated list of Content-Types for which Integration Server
processes an empty payload.  When Integration Server receives a request with an
empty payload and the Content-Type header is specified in
watt.server.content.type.processEmptyPayload, Integration Server processes the
empty payload with the request. For example, if
watt.server.content.type.processEmptyPayload is set to text/plain, when
Integration Server receives a flat file request with an empty payload,
Integration Server places a null ffdata object in the pipeline of the processing
service. If watt.server.content.type.processEmptyPayload does not specify
text/plain, Integration Server does not add an empty object to the pipeline when
receiving a flat file request with no payload. The default value is text/plain. 
 
Do not set this parameter to application/x-www-form-urlencoded, application/xml,
and text/xml as it will result in a SocketTimeOutException when Integration
Server receives requests with one of those Content-Types and with empty
payloads. 
 
You do not need to restart Integration Server for changes to this parameter to
take effect. 

PIE-93849 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Integration Server generates an additional variable if the input for 
a REST API contains a document array at the root level.

For a REST API, if the input includes a document array at the root
level, the pipeline receives an additional variable named $rootArray.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-94248 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)

PIE-94358 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix15)
Beginning with IS_10.15_Core_Fix13, the Dockerfile generated by the is_container
script does not create the sagadmin user as the container user. 
 
Prior to IS_10.15_Core_Fix13, when generating a Dockerfile, the is_container
script created a sagadmin user which had ownership of the files in the Docker
image. This was the default behavior. A user who is logged into the container
created using that image can run commands as the sagadmin user. Beginning with
to IS_10.15_Core_Fix13, the script does not create the sagadmin user. The
generated Dockerfile needs to be modified manually to add the command that
creates the user. While the sagadmin user is not needed to run Integration
Server or Microservices Runtime in a Docker container (Docker runs everything as
root), the existence of the sagadmin user is a convenience. 
 
Now, the is_container script once again creates the sagadmin user by default. If
-Dimage.createUser=false, the is_container script does not create the sagadmin
user. 

PIE-92334 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix14)
Integration Server has a security vulnerability that allows a
Developer user to create a user and grant administrator privileges.

A user with Developer privileges can create a scheduled task using a
built-in service to add a user and run the task, even without permission
to invoke the service. Similarly, the Developer user can add a user
to the Administrators group making Integration Server vulnerable
to security risks.

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server provides the
watt.server.scheduler.checkUserAcl server configuration parameter
to validate a user invoking the service in a scheduled task.

watt.server.scheduler.checkUserAcl
Indicates whether Integration Server verifies if a user has Execute ACL
permission for a scheduler service. Set this parameter to true to enable
the verification or false to disable it. The default value is true.

You do not need to restart the server for the changes to the parameter
to take effect.

PIE-92369 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix14)
The wm.xslt.File:save service in Integration Server has an access control flaw
that exposes the server to security risks.

A developer user has Execute ACL permission for the wm.xslt.File:save service,
allowing the user to perform sensitive administrative tasks, making the server
insecure.

This issue is resolved. Now, only administrator users have the Execute ACL
permissions for the wm.xslt.File:save service.

PIE-93865 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix14)
The pub.report:runTemplate service can return the contents of files located
outside of the specified input package but should not. 

Now the pub.report:runTemplate service can only return the contents of files in
the templates or pub directories for the package specified in the $package input
parameter. 

PIE-83187 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
The pub.document:documentToXMLValues service inaccurately encodes Asian language
characters in the input. 

This issue is now resolved by introducing the
watt.server.support.asianLangCharEncoding server configuration parameter. Set
the parameter to true to ensure that the 
pub.document:documentToXMLValues service properly encodes Asian language
characters in the input. Set the parameter to false to encode Asian language
characters like the rest of the input. 

Note: If your input contains 4-byte Japanese characters, the service 
may not produce the desired output if you do not set the parameter to true.

You do not need to restart Integration Server for changes to this parameter to
take effect. 

PIE-85549 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Integration Server names the root element of REST definitions
in a resource-first REST API Descriptor (RAD) in an unexpected manner.

For a resource-first RAD, if services have associated document types,
Integration Server generates REST definitions for each document type referenced
in the Swagger document. The REST definition is named after the node name of
the document type. For example, if a document type A references document type B
with the variable name abc, the generated Swagger document automatically
generates a request or response for this operation in the Swagger editor. For
XML media types, the root element in the XML is the REST definition name, which
corresponds to the document type name. However, some users might expect the
variable name to be the root element in the autogenerated request or response. 

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server adds an XML tag for the REST
definitions where the XML name property has the value as the variable name
to ensure that the auto-generated root XML name is the variable name and not
the node name. 

PIE-86524 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Docker images for Integration Server and Microservices Runtime in the container
registry now indicate which fixes are installed for the image. 

The Docker images created for Integration Server and Microservices Runtime
available in the container registry at
https://containers.softwareag.com/products now include the readme files for
fixes installed in the image. The readme file are in the SUM readme folder
located at: /opt/softwareag/readme 

PIE-86607 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
After upgrading the Mavericks JAR, Integration Server does not use the
sftpLicenseKey.cnf file in the IntegrationServer\instances\default\config\sftp
folder of the installation. Therefore, the file is removed.

PIE-86812 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Integration Server 10.5 blocks incoming payload requests that include certain
file types (for example, .pdf or .png) within multipart/form-data as SQL
injection violation. 

Integration Server blocks payload requests containing specific file types 
(for example, .pdf or .png) as an SQL injection violation. Moreover, if 
incoming payload requests include such file types within multipart/form-data,
Integration Server 10.5 blocks the request at Enterprise Gateway because
multipart/form-data is not supported by the Enterprise Gateway rules. 

The issue is now resolved. If you want to instruct Integration Server to 
bypass validation for any specific content type against the SQL injection, use 
watt.server.enterprisegateway.SQLinjection.ignoreContentType system
configuration parameter. 

PIE-87359 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Integration Server generates a configuration file for the WmAssetPublisher
package even when the package is unavailable.

Despite safely deleting the WmAssetPublisher package, Integration Server
generates the assetpublisher.cnf file in packages/WmAssetPublisher/config at
some point after restart. However, generating the configuration file when the
package is absent is incorrect. 

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-87543 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Integration Server stores the file path in the "configPassman.cnf" file for an 
encrypted package-level global variable as an absolute file path.

When you define a package-level global variable as a password, Integration 
Server uses a separate configPassman.cnf file within its corresponding package 
folder to specify the name and file path to store the encrypted passwords. The 
file path specified in the configuration file is an absolute file path.
Therefore, when you use the package on a different operating system platform, 
such as Linux, the absolute path specified in the configuration file becomes 
irrelevant, making the package being platform-dependent.

The issue is resolved by changing the file path in the configuration file to a 
relative path.

PIE-87607 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)

When the initial login to Integration Server through LDAP fails due to an

requiring a server restart. However, even after restarting Integration Server, 
the connection is only briefly established before it is lost again.

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-87616 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)

PIE-87813 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Missing response body for undefined HTTP status codes.

When an OpenAPI document specifies a "default" schema for HTTP status codes, the
schema should be used for the response body of any undefined HTTP responses.
Therefore, if the service's output aligns with the default response body for an
undefined HTTP status code, the client should receive this default response
body. However, the response body is missing in such scenarios. 
 
This issue is now resolved.

PIE-87862 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Designer experiences delay while rendering the pipeline view for a map step.

The lack of an option to cache the missing or non-existent nodes 
impacts the performance of Designer while rendering the pipeline 
view for a map step.

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server provides an option 
to enable the cache for non-existent nodes with a cache expiry time.

Note:
Install this fix with the corresponding Designer fix (WED-10465
(ESB_10.11_Fix7)) to resolve the issue.

PIE-88265 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)

PIE-88300 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Integration Server throws an AdminAPIException stating that it cannot initialize
the administrative API for Adapter Runtime even though the WmART package is
disabled or removed. 
 
Integration Server attempts to load the administrative API for Adapter Runtime
even though the WmART package is disabled or uninstalled. When the WmART package
is not available, this causes an AdminAPIException followed by a stack trace to
be written to the server log, specifically: 

com.softwareag.is.admin.AdminAPIException: [ISS.0030.0001]
com/wm/adapters/common/adminapi.json not found. Cannot initialize the
administrative API for Adapter Runtime. 

This has been resolved. If the WmART package is not available, Integration
Server does not attempt to load Adapter Runtime's administrative API. Instead,
Integration Server logs the following message: 

ISS.0030.0038I The administrative API for Adapter Runtime is not present.

PIE-92327 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix13)
Integration Server incorrectly generates referenced objects in a JSON schema.
 
When attempting to import a JSON schema containing an 'enum' field of type
integer, Integration Server fails to recognize the enum type and imports it as
an object. 

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-83648 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)
Change in minimum value for the amount of the JVM to dedicate to the Statistics 
Data Collector.

The luceneMemorySize parameter in the monitor.cnf specifies the number of 
megabytes of memory to dedicate to the Statistics Data Collector. Prior to this 
fix, the minimum value was 256. Now, the minimum is a positive integer.

Note: The default value for luceneMemorySize is 256 MB, which is the recommended 
minimum value. Specifying less memory may cause performance problems or runtime 
errors with the Statistics Data Collector. 
 
The luceneMemorySize parameter corresponds to the Memory size option for the 
Dashboard Configuration in Integration Server Administrator.

For example, 'HTTP/1.1 403 VirusFound' if a virus is found and 'GET / HTTP/1.1'
if a virus is not found.

PIE-86698 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)

PIE-86815 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)
The sample.xslt:transformToString service in the WmXSLT package is susceptible 
to XML External Entity (XXE) injection.

This issue is now resolved by introducing the watt.core.xml.loadExternalEntities 
server configuration parameter with the default value as false. 
If the parameter is set to false, the service ignores any external entities 
referenced in the input.

Note: If the parameter is set to true, the service parses the external entity 
references, which makes Integration Server vulnerable to XXE injection.

You do not need to restart the server for the changes to take effect.

PIE-87136 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)
Integration Server throws an exception while creating a docType from an XML 
schema definition (XSD) due to the absence of prefix for the XML namespace in a 
field within the XSD.

While creating a docType using an XSD extracted from a generated Web Services 
Description Language (WSDL) file, if the XSD has a field that contains the XML 
namespace but without an assigned prefix for the namespace, Integration Server 
throws the following exception:

[ISC.0124.9017] Document to XSD error: Field testField cannot be represented 
in XML Schema. The field contains an XML Namespace property but the field name 
does not contain a prefix.

This issue is resolved by introducing the following server configuration 
parameter.

watt.core.schema.ignoreFieldNamespacePrefix

Specifies whether Integration Server ignores the absence of a prefix for the XML 
namespace in a field within the XSD while creating a docType using an XSD from 
a generated WSDL file. When set to true, Integration Server ignores the absence 
of the prefix, enabling Integration Server to create a docType without any error. 
The default is false.

Integration Server restart is not required for changes to the parameter to 
take effect.

PIE-87316 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)
After PIE-83691 resolution, Integration Server uses the named character entity 
to escape apostrophes while using pub.xml:documentToXMLString, leading to output 
compatibility issues for some users.

After applying a fix that includes the solution for PIE-83691, Integration 
Server uses the named character entity to escape single quotes or apostrophes 
while using pub.xml:documentToXMLString. However, the output format might not be 
suitable to all users.
 
This issue is now resolved by introducing the watt.server.htmlEncode.aposAsEntity 
server configuration parameter, which by default maintains the previous behavior 
of representing apostrophes as the decimal equivalent of the ASCII code rather 
than using the named character entity. When set to true, Integration Server 
encodes single quotes or apostrophes as the named character entity. The default 
value is false.
Integration Server restart is not required for changes to this parameter to take 
effect.

PIE-87505 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)
Addition of configuration variables (application.properties) support for keystore 
and truststore properties.

Microservices Runtime (or an Integration Server with a Microservices license) 
now supports use of the following keys for keystore properties on the Security > 
Keystores >Create/Edit keystore alias pages:

- keystore.<aliasName>.ksDescription: Corresponds to the Description field.
- keystore.<aliasName>.kslsHsm: Corresponds to HSM Based Keystore field. Set to 
true to specify that the keystore is stored on a Hardware Security Module (HSM) 
device. If set to true, the value of the keystore.<aliasName>.location is ignored.
- keystore.<aliasName>.ksType: Corresponds to the Type field. Default supported 
values are: JKS, PKCS12. Other keystore types may be available by loading 
additional security providers, or by setting the watt.security.keyStoreTypes 
server configuration property.
- keystore.<aliasName>. ksStoreProviderName: Corresponds to the Provider field. 
Default supported values are as follows: 
  - If keystore.<aliasName>.ksType  is set to JKS: SUN
  - If keystore.<aliasName>.ksType is set to PCKS12: BC, SUN, SunJSSE

Microservices Runtime (or an Integration Server with a Microservices license) 
now supports use of the following keys for truststore properties in the on the 
Security > Truststores >Create/Edit truststore alias pages:

- truststore.<aliasName>.ksDescription: Corresponds to the Description field.
- truststore.<aliasName>.ksType: Corresponds to the Type field. Default supported 
values are: JKS, PKCS12. Other truststore types can be made available by loading 
additional security providers, or by setting the watt.security.TrustStoreTypes 
server configuration property.
- truststore.<aliasName>.ksStoreProviderName: Corresponds to the Provider field. 
Default supported values are as follows:   
  - If truststore.<aliasName>.ksType  is set to JKS: SUN
  - If truststore.<aliasName>.ksType is set to PKCS12: BC, SUN, SunJSSE

PIE-87548 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)

PIE-87897 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)
Integration Server experiences slow response time for HTTP or HTTPS client calls 
during an SSL connection.

Integration Server performs a reverse DNS lookup for every client request 
before verifying the "Access Mode" setting or the IP access list 
configuration for the global or port IP access delaying the response from 
Integration Server to the client, resulting in slow response time for HTTP or 
HTTPS client calls during the SSL connection.

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server performs a reverse DNS lookup 
only after verifying the "Access Mode" setting and the configuration of 
IP access lists for specific ports or globally.

PIE-87957 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix11)

Integration Server becomes indefinitely unresponsive while obtaining 
a connection from a JDBC connections pool. However, the cause
is untraceable as the server log lacks the information to find processes
that block the database connection.

to help identify the problematic processes.

PIE-82194 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Scheduled tasks in Integration Server are stuck in the Active state with 
Next Run value as 0.0.

When a scheduled task fails to run before the Next Run time elapses, the task 
remains in the Active state with the Next Run value as 0.0, which does not show 
that the scheduled task is delayed.

This issue is resolved. Now, Integration Server provides the 
watt.server.scheduler.nextRun.hidePastValue server configuration parameter 
that specifies how Integration Server displays the elapsed Next Run time for a 
scheduled task that fails to run before the Next Run time elapses. If the 
parameter is set to true, the Next Run time shown as 0.0. 
If the parameter is set to false, the Next Run time is shown with a negative
sign, indicating the delay in running the scheduled task. The default value is 
true.

You do not need to restart the Integration Server for changes to the parameter
to take effect.

PIE-85141 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)

PIE-85362 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)

PIE-85423 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Integration Server incorrectly names the first server log file after
a rollover.

When configuring size-based rollover for server log using the 
watt.server.serverlogRotateSize server configuration parameter, 
Integration Server incorrectly uses the previous day's date in the 
filename of the first log file after the rollover.

This issue is resolved. Integration Server now uses the current date in

PIE-85485 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Integration Server incorrectly sets the default Content-Type header in  
POST or DELETE requests, even when the client does not specify the header.

Despite the absence of the Content-Type header in POST or DELETE requests, the 
pub.client:http service explicitly sets the header to the default value: 
"application/x-www-form-urlencoded". However, according to HTTP 1.1, 
specifying the Content-Type header is optional. Therefore, if the client does
not include the header in the request, the pub.client:http service should not 
add it. 

The issue is now resolved by introducing the
'watt.server.http.setDefaultContentType' 
server configuration parameter, which determines whether Integration Server sets 
the default Content-Type header in the requests. If the parameter value is true, 
Integration Server sets the default Content-Type header in the request even 
though the client does not include it. If the parameter value is false,
Integration Server does not set the default Content-Type header, when it is 
originally absent in the request.

The default value of the parameter is true. However, Integration Server 
automatically sets the Content-Type header to
"application/x-www-form-urlencoded" when data is passed to the pub.client:http 
service using the 'args' or 'table' keys, irrespective of the 
'watt.server.http.setDefaultContentType' parameter value.

You do not need to restart Integration Server for changes to this parameter to
take effect. 

PIE-85560 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
If a java.sql.SQLException repeatedly occurs while the Statistics Data Collector
is processing SQL query results, the Statistics Data Collector might write a
large number of log messages to the server log. 

While processing results from a SQL query, the Statistics Data Collector might
emit many log messages if a java.sql.SQLException is repeatedly raised while
retrieving data  This results in an inordinate number of messages in the server
log such as the following: 

[ISS.0045.0035W] (tid=###) Failed to read SQL rows. Details: [ISS.0045.0158] An
error occurred while attempting to obtain JVM statistics. Repository statistics
will not include some JVM statistics. 

With this fix, the Statistics Data Collector limits the number of log messages
it writes when a java.sql.SQLException occurs when processing SQL query results. 

PIE-85589 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
JMS connection cannot be enabled if it uses a JNDI alias configured to use a
JBoss provider. 

When a JNDI alias is configured to use JBoss as the provider, attempts to enable
a JMS connection that use the JNDI alias fail with the exception
"javax.net.ssl.SSLException: Unsupported signature algorithm:
rsa_pss_rsae_sha256". 

This issue is now resolved. Integration Server successfully starts a JMS
connection alias that uses a JNDI provider configured to use a JBoss provider. 

PIE-85653 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
A call to the /metrics endpoint returns the sag_is_number_nonservice_errors metric   
that incorrectly includes errors related to service failures. 

This issue is now resolved.

PIE-85675 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Security vulnerability during FTP session.
 
During an FTP session (inbound or outbound), Integration Server exposes the
admin and ns folders in packages, making Integration Server vulnerable to a
script injection. 
 
To address this security vulnerability, Integration Server includes a server
configuration parameter to hide the admin and ns folders in all packages. Set
watt.net.ftp.hide.folders to true to hide the admin and ns folders in packages
during an FTP session. Set to false to leave the admin and ns folders visible
during FTP sessions. The default is false to ensure backward compatibility with
existing solutions. 
 
You do not need to restart Integration Server for changes to this parameter to
take effect. 
 
Important! The default configuration of the new watt.net.ftp.hide.folders
parameter does not resolve the security vulnerability. After applying a fix that
includes PIE-85675, you must set watt.net.ftp.hide.folders to true to address
the security vulnerability. It is more secure to set watt.net.ftp.hide.folders
to true. 

PIE-85708 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Integration Server writes a misleading error message to the server log if the
Statistics Data Collector starts before the WmRoot package finishes loading. 
 
During the Integration Server start up sequence, if the Statistics Data
Collector starts before the WmRoot package finishes loading, Integration Server
writes the following misleading message to the server log: 
 
[ISS.0045.0038E] (tid=<threadID>) Unable to save event in table. Details:
Unexpected error accessing the IS JDBC Pools component. Details: Unable to get
the function alias ISDashboardStats configuration. Details: wm.server.jdbcpool 
 
Now, instead of the above error message, Integration Server writes the following
message at the debug level when the Statistics Data Collector starts before the
WmRoot package finishes loading: 
 
[ISS.0045.0364D] (tid=<threadID>) Statistics Data Collector is waiting for
WmRoot package to finish loading. 
 
Integration Server writes the debug message to the server.log periodically until
the WmRoot package finishes loading.

PIE-86114 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
A configuration variables template generated by Microservices Runtime does not
include all properties for an existing proxy server alias. 

Now, the application.properties file generated by Microservices Runtime includes
a property for each proxy server alias field that specifies a value. 

PIE-86115 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Single sign-on (SSO) to Integration Server Administrator for user already
authenticated via a JAAS login module is not available. 

Integration Server Administrator prompts a user for basic authentication even
though authentication was already performed by a JAAS login module. 

To address this issue, Integration Server now includes a server configuration
parameter to allow SSO to Integration Server Administrator via JAAS. 

watt.security.jaas.restrictSSO
Specifies if single sign-on to Integration Server Administrator is supported
when a user has already been authenticated via a JAAS login module. When set to
false, if JAAS authentication succeeds, access to Integration Server
Administrator does not require additional basic authentication credentials. The
Integration Server log in page is skipped and the user is instead redirected to
the Dashboard. When set to true, if JAAS authentication succeeds, the user must
still provide login credentials when attempting to access Integration Server
Administrator. The default is false. 

You must restart Integration Server for changes to this parameter to take
effect.

PIE-86636 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Client applications can now set the User-Agent value that JSONClient sends to
Integration Server. 

When the CSRF Guard feature is enabled on Integration Server and the
watt.net.userAgent property has been changed to something other than the default
value of "webMethods", a call from the JSONClient class to the Integration
Server results in an  HTTP 400 response code. 

To resolve this issue, the following methods have been added to
com.wm.app.b2b.client.JSONClient: 

    public void setUserAgent(String)
    public String getUserAgent()

Client applications that use JSONClient to communicate with Integration Server
can call the setUserAgent method to specify the value that JSONClient will send
in the User-Agent request header. If setUserAgent() is not called, or is passed
null or an empty String, JSONClient will send a User-Agent value of
"webMethods". If Integration Server is using CSRF Guard, client applications
should set JSONClient's User-Agent so that it matches the watt.net.userAgent
setting on the server. If Integration Server has watt.server.http.jsonFormat set
to stream or bytes, the User-Agent value sent by JSONClient must be webMethods.
Client applications can call the getUserAgent method to see what User-Agent
value is currently in use by JSONClient.

PIE-87135 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Integration Server uses SHA-2 instead of PBKDF2 to hash passwords for users
added via application of a configuration variables template. 
 
After applying a fix that includes PIE-85221, Integration Server uses the
Password-Based Key Derivation Function 2 (PBKDF2) hashing algorithm for
passwords for new users. However, Integration Server still uses SHA-2 to hash
passwords for users added via a configuration variables template
(application.properties). This results in Integration Server logging the
following message about a weak password: 
 
[ISS.0012.9999I] (tid=<threadID>) Password stored as weak hash. Consider
updating password to migrate to a stronger hash. 
 
This issue is now resolved.
 
Note: Integration Server converts existing passwords that were hashed using
SHA-2 to a PBKDF2 hash when the password is updated.

PIE-87422 (IS_10.15_Core_Fix10)
Enhancements to gRPC support in Integration Server.

Integration Server now supports the following gRPC features and functionality:

- gRPC field types Enum and Map.
- Custom metadata. A gRPC client and/or server can send gRPC metadata to provide
additional information about the gRPC call, such as custom header information.
At run time, Integration Server places any custom gRPC metadata received for a
gRPC request into a document field (IData object) named Custom-Metadata, adding
one child field for each key-value pair of gRPC metadata. Integration Server
passes the Custom-Metadata field to the input pipeline to the gRPC method flow
service invoked by the RPC call. Your gRPC method flow service can include logic
that makes use of the gRPC metatada. Note: The document types generated for the
gRPC message do not include fields for custom metadata.

were not caused by ServiceExceptions. 
- sag_is_package_load_error - Name of a package that had errors when loading.
